est dominus et egestate compulsus furer et periurem nomen dei mei beggery sayth richesse ne gyue thou gyue thou oonly lyuelode nedefull thynges lest perauenture fulfylled drawen denye saye lorde compelle hym stele neyther forswere hym whiche prayer refuseth noo pouerte dooth habondauce richesse prayer indyfferentely beholdeth grete richesse moche pouerte also syr saaf thy pacyence thou rehersest wordes salomon prayer false englysshe conuenyent sayd gyue neyther richesse ne beggerye thou saydeste sayd gyue rychesse beggerye saye gyue richesse nygardshyppe straytnesse herte couetyse whiche make riche man alwaye begge craue sayd ecclesiastes v ca nygarde hath neuer ynough soo wordes prayeth god yf gyue hym richesse sholde gyue hym therwith largenesse herte grace spende goddes worshyppe haue good good lyfe sayth ecclesiastes vi grete myschyue grete vanyte god gyueth man richesse goodes ynoughe wyll haue gyueth hym power nygardshyp haue parte therof kepeth theym straunger whiche shall deuoure getteth moche care ayenst myschyef beggery couetyse salomon made prayer sayenge lorde gyue richesse beggerye togyder suche nygardshyppe beggerye maketh riche men forsake theyr god vnderstonde beggerye pouerte ye cometh myscouetyse pouerte beggerye cometh nede wantynge good riche man nedeth begge bodely poore pdiues false ppauper preue dauyd worthy kynge sayd ego autem mendicus sum et parper sayd begger poore man glose sayth thus beggyng axe thynge hath hym selfe riche man nedeth poore axe helpe shewed afore ergo nedeth hym begge poore man pdiues alle though axe helpe men v nedeth yet paye theym theyr trauaylle theyr good therfore noo beggerye couenaunte makynge payeng byeng sellynge ppauper full ofte ye paye full euyll thou askeste loue penye poore nedy man axeth loue god thou profferest men whome thou axest bodely helpe penye theyr nede god prouffereth hym selfe mede theym helpe poore men pdiues beggers goostly sayth saynt austyn haue noo good goostly goddes gyfte ppauper ergo beggers bodely haue noo good bodely goddes gyfte caplm ix diues thy speche resonable moche pleasaunt many riche folke praye thy name ppauper askest thou pdues twenty yere goo spake man thyn astate full lyke speche persone spake hygh perfeccyon thou begynnest doo vnto daye coude neuer atteyne therto tolde tale yonge man thou toldest ppauper whicht yonge man pdiues hy asked cryste sholde haue blysse withouten ende whome cryste taught hym perfeccon thou spekest yet dyde doo ppauper ther two maner perfeccyons whiche cryste spake taught yt yonge riche man ther perfeccyon lesse perfeccon fyrste nedefull suffycyent seconde passyng holynesse full excellent fyrste god sayth perfectus eris sine macula glosa criminali deu xviij thou shalt sayth perfyte without spotte dedely synne perfeccyon spake cryste yonge riche man whan bad hym kepe comaudementes seconde perfeccon soo excellent sayd hym si vi perfectus esse yf thou wylt perfyte go selle thou haste gyue poore folke come folowe pdiues tale tolde thy brother twenty yere paste spake moost hygh perfeccyon excellencye praye lete v speke whyle lesse perfeccyon nedefull sythen may atteyne perfeccyon wolde muste kepe holde well lesse perfeccyon ppauper cryste taughte yonge riche man serua mandata kepe well commauadementes haue one god worshyppe take name ydelnesse halowe holy dayes fader moder worshyppe paye slee noo blysse yu louest thy selfe hym yu woldest men dyde hym yu woldest men dyde longe kepeth lawe charyte yf forfete ayenst charyte charyte chastyse hym punysshe hym tyll wyll amende hy saluacon soule wryte gen erthe byddynge god brought forth tree grasse herbes tree herbes brought forth theyr fruyte eche theyr owne kynde thyrde daye er god made sonne mone sterres badde erthe gaue vertue nature wonderfull nature bud brynge forth leues fayre grene dyuerse fourme floures fayre blossomes bryghte dyuerse shappe dyuerse colour noo man crafte deuyse also gaue nature brynge forth fruyt fayre fyne wytchecraftes may tolde specyall praye telle generall wytchecraft ppauper euery craft man woman vseth knowe ony thyng ony thyng may knowe ne waye reason ne werkyng kynde wytchecrafte though waye kynde vse therto ony charmes nyce obseruau ce doynge wenynge myght done without charme suche obseruaunce ellys suche charmes oonly blynde people sholde truste hym charmes werkyng kynde wytchecrafte yf say pater noster doynge holden charmer people truste hym pryncypally charmes though sayth charmes werketh kynde yet wytche doynge wytche crafte suche doynge blyndeth people dysceyued doth truste wytchecrafte worshyp fende despyte god euer man woman waye kynde reason yf vse ony crafte iapery faytrye blynde people byleue wytche dyde waye kynde charmes sorcery wytche goddes syght doynge wytchecrafte crafte make men worshyppe fende moche doth people truste wytchecrafte spende theyr good fendes seruyce seke helpe fende forsake goddes helpe hath leuer hym selfe holden wytche deuylles seruaunte holden goddes seruaunte leuer take mennes good worshyppynge fende worshyppyng god connynge grace god hath gyuen hym myght vertue god hath gyuen thynges kynde helpe mannes kynde falsely enhaunceth fendes crafte destruccyon mankynde pdiues tell example ppauper hele mannes woundes whyle fresshe clene blacke wulle oyle ben full medycynable without ony charme experyence sheweth well moche men wene nought worthe without charme sette theyr fayth pryncypally charme therfore wytche crafte though man doyng say pater noster holy prayer callynge grace god doynge noo wytche crafte well fastynge sholde deye sodaynly haue tyme repentauce shreuen houseled sholde rechelesse theyr lyuynge sholde lesse care doo amys hope amendemente theyr dyeng therfor god grau teth ende effecte faste greter sodayne deth wyste neuer men wyste theym haue haue fasted suche fastes vij yeres ne dyspytefull shame full open punysshyng theyr synne ther neuer soo moche sodayne deth longe reygnyng londe ben colde kynde dreme frostes snowe theyr dremes wyse leche may knowe parte dysposycon ther bodye helthe sekenes thyrde cause inwarde dysposycon ye soule comonly men dremen suche thynges ther soules theyr thoughte moost occupyed whyle yt waken eyther studye loue hate wrath drede sorowe care pryde couetyse cause dremes outwarde ben two maner bodely ghoostly bodely dysposycon ayer place hym thynges besyde hym therfore rayne weder men dreme water fysshes ofte mane bodye chaugeth dysposycyon ayer abydynge place thre cause sayth phylosophre de somno et vigilia lech sholde take bede dremes ben seke vident pdiues sayste thou whan go huntynge passe waye yf mete man holy chirche relygyon namely frere wyl leue hym theyr lyfte honde wene spede better worse yf leue hy theyr right honde ppauper saye prophete tu nobis e dne et nomen sanctum tuum inuocatum est super no ne derelinquas no dne deus noster ieremye xiiij lorde sayth thou arte amonges v lorde amonges seruauntes thyn holy name called vpon fendes seruauntes take goddes name vayne grete despite goddes name therfor cryste sayth suche wycked crysten people per vos tota die nome meu blasphemat genti bus ysaye lij et ad ro ij name despysed charge customably falsely wote well swereth false dyspyteously dysceyuable swereth ony creature vseth ony nyce othes vnlefull othes take goddes name vayne ought noo man ne woman swere treuthe charge whan nedeth swere wytnesse treuthe whan man shall swere shall swere god noo creature pdiues moche folke brought custome swerynge vnnethe speke thre wordes togydre swere god creature grete nyce othe ppauper sayd fore wycked custome excuseth synne accuseth aggregeth synne therfore drede yt yt swere customably soo lyghtly synne dedely yf swere soth false therfore salomon sayth iuracioni ne assuescas o tuu eccle xxiij lete thy mouthe sayth vseth swerynge many harde happes fallynges ben suche swerynge name ofte sayth goddes name thy mouth swerynge ne vsaunt swerynge medle sayntes name yf thou thou shalte clere fole swerynge ne clere synne man sayth yt swereth moche shalbe fulfylled synne shrewednesse trybulacon dysease shal passe fro hym housholde god sayth taketh name vayne shall passe vn punysshed suche swerynge despysynge goddes name horryble synne goddes syght salomon sayth boke xxvij ca whan men herde suche swerynge theyr hedes sholde aryse drede sholde stoppe theyr eres loue haue god haue hym often mynde saye may swere swere soth saye swere ther wyll man byleue ppauper ben excusacons greuous accusacons grutchynges synne fyrste poynte false suche false swerers loue theyr god kepe comaundement haue hym full lytyll mynde swere many horryble othes vanyte shrewednesse bycause mysuse whan thynke god therfore excusacon open scorne grete blasphemynge god yf thy seruaunt hadde done thynge thou haddest hym forboden ofter dyde worse thou woldeste payed yf scorned sayd dyde thy loue haue mynde thou woldest holde full grete scorne ben moche angred hym namely yf thou ware lyege lorde kyng moche god lorde kyng thynges angred swere ayenste comaundement excuse scornfully saynge yt haue god mynde therfore drede yt shalbe put mynde amonge goddes chosen people cryste complayneth hym suche folke fader heuen sayth thus qm que tu cussisti secuti sut et su dolore vulner meo rum addiderut fader heuen sayth asmoche wycked swerers haue pursued smyten hym theyr wycked tongue thou sendeste suffre deth saluacon mankynde put newe sorowe aboue sorowe bytter paynes woundes suffred synne theyr sake therfore fader putte synne synne saye lette theym falle fro synne synne lette entre thy rightwysnesse saued put theym boke lyfe amonge theym shall blysse without ende lette theym wryten rightwysse folke shall saued ben crystus wordes complanynge hym fader heuen suche foule swerers po lxviij pdiues semeth herby suche sweryng fulgrete horryble synne full peryllous sayst yu seconde excusacon ppauper ben bounde neuer lye nothyng saye soth neuerthelesse boude saye al sothes ne ought swere euery soth speke sayth saynt thomas de veritate theologie bothe forswereth hym ayenst treuthe swereth treuthe without grete cause take goddes name vayn forswereth wyttyngly name souerayne treuthe yt god despyseth swereth grete cause taketh name ydlenesse swereth without gode cause whan hym nedeth lytyll nought sette goddes name take vayne caplm vi diues many cause lefull swere ppau vij case clerkes lewde folke may swere lefully fyrste saue man woman harme theyr bodye fro lesynge good whan treuthe none wyse preued also confyrmacon pea also kepe fayth treuthe amonge mankynde also kepe obedyence ordynall subgeccyon subgettes theyr soueraynes also saue fredom holy chirche also purgacyon saluacyon mannes name fame also assoylynge curse extra lii de elect significasti euery othe men muste haue thre thynges whiche ben treuthe dome rightwysnesse sayth prophete ieremye iiij shall swere muste haue treuthe co scyence wote wel yt swereth treuthe yf syker weneth syker shal swere yt weneth sayth also muste haue hym dome good dyscrete auysemet er swere swere treurhe nede whome swereth wyll ellys byleue hym thynges charge prouffytable byleued swere also muste haue rightwysnesse thynge swereth maner sweryng rightfull honest lefull extra liij de iure iurando et si xps pdiues wolde fayne flee suche othes sayd fyrste men wyll bylene swere ppau yf treuthe charge right profytable byleued men wyl byleue thy symple worde leful swere haue sayd yf thyng charge nenedefull swere yu yf thou vse swere comonly thynge nought thou synnest greuously makest wanbyleue yt sholde nomore byleue thyn othe without othe wyse men wyl lesse byleue thyn othes comonly grete swerers vsaunt swerers ben full false pdiues ppauper take goddes name vayne ben false god theyr swerynge sythen ben false god theyr swerynge gyue lytyll tale false man woma theyr swerynge begyle othes therfore yf yu wylt men byleue ye nay vse speke truly dyscretly flee othes worshyp goddes name true god byeng sellynge speche lyuynge men sholde byleue redely without ony othe doo soo speke men may holde trewe man men shall byleue ye nay better theyr greter othes yf thou varyenge vntrusty thy worde thy dede men wyll neyther byleue othe neyther without othe pdiues therfore saye cryste forbade maner sweryng whan hae sayd gospell ego aute dico vobis iurare oino mathei v saye ye swere wyse ppau englysshe crystus worde englysshe saye ye swere ony maner saye maner cause lyghtly ne customably also badde tho wordes men sholde swere creature wytnes neyther heuen goddes trone ne erthe stole vnder fete ne ierlm cyte grete kyng ne thyne hede thou canste make one thyn here whyte ne blacke lete worde ye ye nay nay mathei v pdiues muste saye twyes ye twyes nay ppauper yu must yf yu wylt true ye thou sayste thy mouth yu muste saye thyn herte thy mouth thyn herte muste accorde togydre yf thou saye ye thy mouth nay thyn herte yu arte false doste ayenst crystus lore pdiues yet contra te saynt iames sayth ante oia fres mei nolite iurare iacobi v byfore thynges leue brethern wyll ye swere neyther heue ne erthe ne ony othe wherby semeth lefull swere ppauper saynt iames forbedeth v vtterly swere byddeth men sholde wyll swere ony othe men sholde swere nede pdiues yet contra te cryste byddeth gospell mathei v worde sholde ye ye nay nay qd aute habundanci est malo est speche full euyll wherby semeth yf men say ye nay othes swerynge amys ppauper cryste sayd euyll saye ye nay swere whan nedeth sayd full euyll men swere saye ye nay cometh wanbyleue hym wyl byleue euen crysten swere also cometh falshede people moche people false vnnethe men may byleue theym without othe othe pdiues fyndeste yu god badde men swere leful swere ppauper gospell yu allegest ayenst mathei v cryste swere sayth theyr saye hym credence reuerence ben selfe god dygnyte ordre kynde man bothe god man therfore wyll take swerynge wytnesse hym souerayne treuthe therfore suche maner swerynge dyuyne byndeth hym selfe leyeth hede thedame plegge god prayeth god leese hede thedame neuer thryue sayth sayth behoteth swere theyr soule theyr chaffre goodes haue bynde theym lese theyr soule theyr chaffre wherfore iewe chalenged golde ye crysten man byfore iuge sayd falsely payed hym whan iuge sholde sytte cause crysten man bethought hym begyle fayned hym seke cam lenyng staffe byfore iuge whiche one dyd soone stale oxe take ledde galowes fende mette hym sayd hym wheder awaye theef sayd fende woo worth wycked wyght yu haste brought ende sayd fende blame thou myghtest see byll goo caplm viij diues suppose man haue borowed thynge lent hym taketh awaye fro hym preuely ayenst wyll ayenst couenau lenynge doth man theft takyng away owne good ppauper doth theefth yt tyme fully owne good raymude sayth liij ti de furtis yf lord lady ony man betake seruaut offycer ony thynge kepe take away fro hym without wetynge false couety se malyce endaugere seruaut doth theft though thynge owne yet frely owne longe seruaut assent hath kepynge dyspensacon therof pdiues suppose weneth take owne good whan taketh mane good ayest wyll yf take owne good vnlefully wenynge yt lefull take dooth ony theeft case ppauper nay though case vnlefully yet case doth theft ne dedely synne yet boude restytucon theeft encludeth alwaye gyle falsenes wt whiche theft yf man take mannes good wyttynge yf haue iuste cause wene yt sholde myspayed tho wyste doth theft ne synne yf take mane good wenynge yt wyll tho wyl yt take yet doth theft dedly synne goddes syght boude restytucon whan knoweth yt yt lordes wyll ne lorde may axe restytuco n syth wyl yf man woman mys eggynge take awaye mane seruaut doth theft yf man selle bye man woman yt fre gyuet hym taketh hym gyft ayensthys wyl doth theft sayth raymu vbi su yf man woman take prysoner tyme ryghtfull batayl fre therfor mayster may gyue selle hym lawe armes wa e hy lawe conscyence charyte pdiues yf man haue hyred borowed hors ony thynge certayn place certayn tyme passe yt place tyme ayenst wyll ought yt thynge doth theeft ppauper yf purpo se couetyse euyll cause doth theft yf falle sodayne case whan cometh place hyred knewe case whan hyred thynge muste nedes perfourme case ellys falle grete harme may take horse thynge ferther lenger without theeft may truly paye passeth fyrste couenau pdiues yf man lene awaye mannes good without assent hym whiche good lent vse ppauper doth theft haue iuste cause wene yt lorde yt thynge shal myspayd yt lenynge vseth mane good ayenst wyl lucre wynnynge frendshyp yf man lene ony thynge vpon wed vsed wed without leue hym ought doth theeft saluacon thyng yf vse sparyng owne good lucre fals couetyse ayenst wyll yt ought doth theft sayth clerke yf thyng stolen perysshe though thefe haue fyte therby yet bou de restytucyon muste yelde good better whan toke boude make restytuco n yt thynge profyte yt cam therof hy yt profyte sholde haue come therof lorde tyme yt occupyed ayenst wyl yf haue amended thynge yt stale may axe ayen ne withholde expense shal make restytucon thynge worth whan stale better yf theef profre lorde couenable tyme place stolen thynge lord wyll receyue yf thyng yt myshap perysshe lorde hath none accyon ayenst theef lettynge restytucon ne profyte myght haue come therof profred hym tyme byfore yf man haue stolen thynge boude restytucon yt thynge also value vse pdiues yf man woman bye open market thynge stolen wenynge stolen whan knoweth sothe may axe pryce yt thynge hym ought withdrawe tyll haue payed hy moche payde therfore ppau reymude clerkes saye nay therfor beware tyme losse also suspeccon theft lyghtly beggyg stolen thyng myght take theef nethelesse may ryghtfully axe payment hym solde hym whan hath restored lorde yt thynge yf spent ony thynge amendement yt thyng whyle ayen euen value yf take ouer vse doth vsure boude restytuco n pdiues contra god gaaf leue iewes take vsure nacons ppauper flee euyll el wolde haue taken vsurye theyr brethern couetyse god forbadde graunted take vsure nacyons amonge spare theyr owne nacon also gete ayen parte yt longed ye graut god al londe enhabyte wt hethen people longed ye iewes ye graut god wrongfully ye hethen peple withelde moche londe fro caplm xxv lordes mylles lene moneye baker folke couenaut shal grynde theyr mylles vsurye let theym yt may grynde frely wyl yf harmed therby leners bouden make restytucon yf harmed therby boude restytucon let theyr fredom somdele bouden chapman selle creaunce let byer chapman bycause lenynge selle derer suche seller ben bouden restytucyon byer harmed hyndred yf lener ony man wyll gyue dettour lenger tyme paymet whan may kepe daye assygned haue gyft though axe gyft openly doth vsure yf chapman selle derer lenynge pryce sholde selle yf payed anone doth vsure bouden restytucyon extra lieti consuluit yf borower vpon vsure fayle daye payment borowe may paye moneye vsure lener dettour whome borowe paye hym ayen moneye vsure borowe none vsure wynneth nought therby fleeth myscheue sholde elles falle hym yf man compelled borowe moneye vsure falsehede dettour wyl paye terme false dettour bounden make restytucyon det also vsure compelled paye falsehede el delyuer hym dauger yf yet paye extra liiijde fideiussori bus cauenit et ca constitutus yf man woman lene x shellynges eester tyme resceyue many busshelles whete myghelmasse whete better yt tyme moneye doubte reasonably whether whete shall worthe lesse tyme payment none vsure yf semely sholde worthe tyme payment lent moneye hope lucre dyd vsure extra e ti nauigantiet su confliijtivij yf seller selle thynge pryce cause abydeth paye dooth vsure yf byer bye thynge lesse worth payeth byfore thynge bought may taken hym doth vsure ibidem suma conf yf man lene syluer wyne haue ayen quantyte certayn tyme hope yt quantyte shall worth tyme paymet doth vsure yf dettour wyl paye hym det byfore tyme flee owne harme wyll take hym tyme assygned payment wynne lenynge dooth vsurye yf man lene moneye resceyue certayn tyme corn wyne thynge herfore shall take moche cometh therto tyme payment yf man lene moneye resceyue maner moneye therfor certayn tyme wynne therby soo charge dettour doth vsurye yf man selle thynge certayn pryce market goth tyme sellynge couenaut yf better worth byfore cester shal paye moche though lesse worth shall paye lesse doth vsurye yf byer bye horse bestis lesse pryce worth tyme byenge resceyue theym certayn tyme feyre vsure wene sykerly sholde moche worth lesse worth yf wene sholde tyme worth vsurye caplm xxvi yf man let horse oxe cowe hyre couenaut beste dye appeyre hyreth shall stande losse halfe wynnynge yf amende doth vsurye semely sholde haue moche profyte amendement beste sholde haue harme deth nathelesse though letteth hyre make suche couenaut hym hyreth hym besy saue beste doth synne yf purpose take though beste perysshe without defaute yf gyle couetyse doth vsurye therfor good flee suche couenauntes alle though entencyon good yet maner couenaunt semeth wycked sclaunderous folke knowe entencyon nathelesse hyreth thynge may lefully take hym peryll myscheef thynge hyreth yf wyl yf man betake beest poore man hyre kepe couenaunt vtterly yf dye shall dye poore man lyue hym wyll haue good therfor wycked vsurye suche vsurers ben fendes charmours suche folke theyr shepe ne theyr bestes shall neuer dye yf men tyme plente bye corne nedefull thynges pryncypally selle theym forth derer tyme derthe nede synne yf pryncypaly comon profyte saluacyon contree medefull ioseph gouernour egypt dyde saue people tyme hongre gen xlvij also man maye owne psofyt flee myscheef comyng waye prouydence though selle forth tyme nede helpe market goth doth synne yt yf witholde wyl selle forth tyme nede thyng hath passyng lyuyng kepeth stylle hope derth synneth greuously therfore salomon sayth qui abscondit frumentu maledicet populis bndictio dni su caput vendenciu prouerbio rum xi hydeth whete tyme hongre shall accursed amonges people blessynge god vpon hede selle forth also may done comon ryght marchaundyse wynne therby ther true lyuynge soo cause derthe ther byenge namely may bye lefully haue wherby lyue suche marchaudyse yf auaryce compelle men bye men ther lykynge dere wyll synne greuously namely couetou se clerkes haue ynough el wherby lyue clerkes graunted suche marchaundyse yf clerke bye beest thynge husbondrye craft lefull hym amended put better degree byfore maye selle forthe lefully bought suche doynge called proprely crafte marchaundysexxiiijqiij canonu glosa et de condiv nun yf man lene olde corne haue therfore newe corne heruest wyll take olde corne olde corne good good whan borower maye paye doth vsurye raymunde sayth et suma confes vbi supra yf done pryncypally saue owne good el sholde perysshe pryncypaly helpe neyghboure dooth none vsurye goddes lawe vsurye dampned emperours lawe mannes lawe tyme suffreth good ne lefull flee euyll ofte men sholde perysshe myght borowe vpon vsurye elles couetous ryche men wyl lene nedefull lawe man ryghtfully suffereth good ende couetouse man dooth vnryghtfully wycked ende therfor holy chirche dampneth lene vpon vsurye borowe nede good cause vpon vsurye whan may el borowe yf borowe wycked cause playe dyce spende glotonye lecherye pryde wycked vse synne greuously though lefull borowe good ende vpon vsurye yet leful lene vpon vsurye ne counseyll ony borowe vpon vsurye lefull crysten man take hethen man swereth fals god yet lefull crysten man axe hym othe ne styre hym therto othe swerynge dyuyne worshyp longeth verry god also notaryes make instrumentes vpon couenautes vsurye ben forsworne whan made notaryes make othe shall neuer make instrumentes vpon couenanutes vsurye soo yf make ony suche instrumentes ben forsworne may neuer bere wytnesse ony cause ne make instrumentes ony cause ben made therby wycked name vnable euery fyce worshypfull lawe euery dygnyte ony prelate vnder wrytte suche couenaut sette seale therto wyttyngly gylty vsurye though haue wynnynge therby hec suma confes caplm xxvij diues payne ordeyned lawe vsurers ppauper vsurers lawe ben bounden restytucyon yf ben open vsurers ben accursed lawe thre thynges sholde houseled ne holy chirche shall take ther ferynge ne resceyue crysten buryenge amende byfore theyr deth preest elles taketh offryng buryed shall make restytucon taketh bysshoppe helpe poore folke worthy suspended offyce masse extra eti quia omni bus yf vsurer may make restytucyon muste axe forgyuenesse theym dettour yf wyll saued vsurer also heyre bounden restytucyon may compelled lawe restytucyon extra etitu no yf men bouden hym vsurye may restytucyon axe tyll haue made restytucyon bounde vsurye extra etiquia frustra pdiues wherby sholde men knowe open vsurer pauper kepe open stacyon open shoppe lene chaunge vsurye yf knowlege byfore iuge dome conuycte wytnesse yf bere name vsurer dedes openly done accordynge name clerke vsurer heyre vsurer wyll make restytucon shall suspended wyll amende hym shall deposed yf soo incorrygyble bysshop may amende hym shall chastysed seculer honde extraliijtide iudicijs cacu non ab homine clerke shall make restytucyon owne good yf haue wherof goodes holy chirche yf haue ought spent suche vsurye profyte holy chirche prelate resceyue offerynge vsurer clerkes saye shall take ayen vsurer repreef synne saye shall take bysshoppe whiche shall take ayen vsurer yf vsurer may founden bysshop shall gyue poore folke borower swere shall paye vsurer axe ayen mu e paye saue othe shall axe ayen may make denuncyacon prelate holy chirche v rye vsurer may compelled lawes holy chirche amende hym make restytucyon yf swere shall neuer bewraye holy chirche vsurye bou den othe ayenst saluacyon euen crysten ayenst comaundement god vsurer bye horse londe without moneye vsurer gyue resceyueth gyfte bouden make restytucyon yf wyste soo bought gyuen extra ecu tu seruautes labourer serue vsurers honeste thynges maye lefully take theyr hyre theym yf serue theym thynges nedefull ne lefull may take theyr hyre vsurer yf seruaunt borowe moneye vpon vsurye without byddynge mayster though borowe nedes mayster ony man borowe moneye vpon vsurye nedes without byddynge boroweth bounden restytucyon yf vsurer wolde lene without vsure freely couseylleth hym lene vpon vsure boude restytucon letteth proufyte neyghbour yf iewe lene crysten man vpon vsurye synneth may compelled prelate lordes make restytucon extra e post miserabile lefull ony crysten man woman take vsurye ony man crysten hethen lorde college man sholde suffre vsurers dwelle theyr lordshyp ne lete theym hyre dwelle within thre monethes knowe theyr vsurye sholde put theym neuer resceyue suche vsurers yf bysshop archebysshop doo contrarye ben suspended ben lesse degree ben accursed yf doo contrarye college comontees falle interdyte yf stande stylle theyr malyce one moneth theyr londes ben interdyted lewde people suffre suche vsurers dwelle theyr lordshyp theyr house sholde compelled censure holy chirche put dm grego decimu et consiliu lugdunense ti de vsuris ca vsura rum hec summa confe liijticodem also yf man selle thynge moche lesse worthe couenaunt haue ayen tyme wyll paye pryce worthe vsurye byer getteth ayen payde moche therto yf man selle thynge x shellynges well worth xx shellynges shal haue ayen byer wynneth vsure x shellynges ouer payed fyrste caplm xxviij bvt suche reason many ben wryten false vsurers cursed god begyle robbe poore people ayenst comaundement god sayth thus yf thou lene poore people yu shalt therfore mysbede hym ne trauayll hym therfore ne suche god gyueth curse w sayth ioyne house house couple felde felde saye ryght wronge wronge ryght put lyght derknesse derknesse lyght bytter swete swete bytter ysayev false men lawe slyght couetouse enemyes theft achor stale ayenst goddes byheste god sayd tyll whan thefte punysshed people sholde neuer haue spede batayle ne iourneye pdiues lytell wondre folke spede euyll dayes warre vpon theyr enemyes go robbe pyle fyght ony ryght ppauper synne many spede full euyll blent synne yt lyght grace whiche sholde wyssed ther dedes hyde awaye fro wandre forth amonge theyr enemyes blynde bestes sene myscheef tyll falle wyse man sayth obcecauit eos malicia eo rum sap ij ther malyce hath made theym blynde grete clerke telleth solinus de mirabilibus mundi londe sardynye welle whiche welle yf true man drynke syght shall amende yf theef drynke therof though syght byfore neuer clere shall wexe blynde welle vnderstande plentee worldely goodes rychesses ye god sendeth amonges mankynde whiche goodes rychesses comen erth newen yere yere water welle al true folke drynken welle saye comen truly theyr good rychesses worlde spenden well worshyp god profyte theyr euen crysten haue lyght grace see doo may please god falsely come goodes worlde theeft gyle vsure fals othes wexen blynde lese lyght grace blent wt ther malyce therfore saynt ambrose su luca sayth tyche ss blame blame defaute theym wel vse theyr rychesses rychesses sayth lettynge vertue shrewes helpe vertue good folke ben wyll vse well rychesses pdiues drede nyghe nacyon hath soo dronken welle sardynye ben goostly blynde yf take feldes heyres ieremie viij prophete ysaye god vndernameth gouernoures people bothe temporalyte spyrytualyte sayth thus principe tui infideles socij furum et cetera thy prynces ben false felowes theues louen gyftes folowe medes yeldynge ayen demed ryght men myght paye ysa si videbas furem currebas cu eo et cu adulteris porcionen yf thou see theef thou ranne hym helpe hym false iuges temporalte done dayes lechoures auouteres thou puttedeste thy parte iuges spyrytualte done dayes phere endeth seuenth comaundement begynneth eyght capitulum primu diues full moche drede gyle falsehede shal vndo londe yu sayest god mercy doo bote thanke myne herte thou haste well enfourmed kepynge seuenth comaundement praye charyte yu wylt enfourme eyght commau dement ppauper eyght commaundement non loqueris contra hydynge treuthe whan sholde sayd lawe sayth qui tacet consentire videtur styll wyll saye treuthe whan sholde saye semeth consenteth falsenesse soo stylnesse wytnesseth falsenesse ayenst treuthe ayenst neyghbour synneth dedely tonge wyll vse wytnesse treuthe whan sholde therfore sayth saynt austen bothe hydeth treuth lyeth ayenst treuth ben gylty ayenst comaudement stylle wyll proufyte euen crysten lyeth desyreth harme euen crysten epla ad casulanu man woman bouden comaudement harme neyghbour tonge therfore iohn crysostome sayth traytour treuthe lyeth ayenst treuthe also sayth frely treuthe ought saye frely defendeth treuth whiche ought mayntene defende tho styllenesse enforce theym knowe treuthe yt knowe wyll aknowen due tyme lyers false wytnesses nathelesse leue frende ye shall vnderstande ther thre maner stylne sse one anentes god anentes euen crysten thyrde anentes selfe fyrste wycked whan cesse due praysynge god thankynge benefyces seconde wycked whan cesse due maner techynge vndernemynge euen crysten thyrde wycked ij maners fyrste yf man woman drede shame pryde wyll saye thynge sholde saye playne hym myscheef seke helpe soule shryf good couseyll bodye helpe good couseyll gnawynge fretynge hymselfe inwarde wyll playne hym outwarde wolde conforte hym speketh moche inwarde without conforte tyl falleth wanehope shendeth hymselfe angre inwarde sorowe therfore sayth saynt gregory li viij moraliu moche folke whan haue wronge suffren moche dysease inwarde wyll speke outwarde sayth yf sayd peasably theyr dysease outwarde theyr tonge sorowe dysea se sholde passe theyr herte theyr conscyence si illatas inquit molestias lingua tranquilie diceret consciencia dolor maneret somtyme men stylle desceyte may bodely accuse caplm ij diues many maner ben lesynges pauper saynt austen li de mendaco putteth vij maner lesynges whiche ben comprehended thre quia one mendaciu vel e niciosu vel officio su vel iocosu euery lesynge suche doth harme called latyne niciosu saye wycked englysshe suche doth good none harme called latyn officiosu profytable englysshe suche dooth neyther good ne harme called latyn ocosum bourdfull englysshe whan men make lesynges make folke mery fyrste maner called niciosu wycked alwaye dedely synne two maner lesynges ben venyall synne comon people men holy chirche relygyouse sholde folke perfeccon ben dedely synne yf ben done auysement custome saynt austen sayth fyrst maner lesynges done fyue maners fyrste yf ony man saye preche teche ony thynge ayenst ye fayth holy chirche ij whan lesynge harmeth profyteth none lesynges bacbytynge fals wytne sse synne comon lawe punysshed iij profyteth one harmeth fals wytnesse cause dette herytage suche iiij whan lesynge made without profyt without cause saue lykynge lye desceyue custome lesynges v whan lesynge made please flaterynge alle maner lesynges ben forboden comaundement mener folke dedely synne lesynge flaterynge maye done thre maners praysynge man thynge hath worthy praysed praysyng hym thynge hath praysynge hym flaterynge hy synne shrewednesse folye maner flateryng yf done wyttyngly dedely synne secode maner lesynge called officio su profytable done iij maners fyrste saluacon catel sholde ellys loste wyckedly theues yf wyste also saluacon man woman nocent sought enemyes also saue man woma fro synne yf syngle woman saye wyfe kepe clene theym wolde defoule suche maner lesynges auayle profyte also lesynges bourdfull ben venyal synnes ye comon people men perfeccon ben dedly synne namely lesynges bourdfully whan ben customable vse falleth men holy chirche relygyon iapers ne lyers falleth pryncypally flee ydell wordes cryste sayth gospel men shall gyue answere euery ydell worde saye suche lesynges bourdful men perfeccon tourne lyghtly lesynges nycyous wycked harme theym yt yt asclaudred theyr vanyte theyr lesynges thynketh soth men holy chirche perfeccyon sholde iapers ne lyers ne vayne sadde chere worde dede therfore mayster sentence li iij distinct xxxviij sayth openly yt suche maner lesynges ben venyal synnes vnperfyte state dedly synne perfyte state saynt austyn li tra mendaciu sayth yt teruth sholde corrupte ony temporall profyte man shewed outwarde fer fro ther fayth therfore shewed hym outwarde strauger pylgryme passynge knewe hym ne byleued hym stedfastly also yt doynge shewed sholde passe forth bodely worlde goo aboue heuens pdiues fynde gen xxvij iacob desceyte fader yt blynde fraude brother esau sayd ysaac fader haue blyssynge esau thy fyrste sone false yet god approued dede therfore semeth euery lesynge synne ppauper iacob dyd fygure prophecye thynge sholde falle prophecye done dede therfore lesynge thoughe fyrste sone byrthe yet fyrste sone dygnyte ordynauce god ordeyned people comynge iacob sholde souerayne people comynge esau grete byhest crystus byrth made abraham ysaac sholde fulfylled iacob esan theyr fader wende yt sholde haue though esau fyrste sone pryncypall ysaac dome ysaac yet iacob fyrste sone iacob dede ne speche iacob dede speche holy goost wrought hy spake hym therfore cryste sayd dyscyples ben ye speke holy goost fader heuen speketh spake iacob rebeca mod couseyled hym gete faders austen sayth libro tra men daciu mouth bereth wytnesse herte therfore yf man woman saye otherwyse herte bereth false wytnesse ayenst hert ayenst hymselfe doth ayenst comaudement god byddeth hy saye sworne partye bere wytnesse treuth partye othe vnlefull therfore withstandynge othe may bere wytnesse treuthe intumauit noo man shall bere wytnesse cause yf haue cause ony lyke spede hymselfe suche persone suspecte wolde fauoure mannes cause haue hym fauorable hym cause eti persona noo mannes wytnesse shall resceyued dome preiudyce yf swere though wytnesse man relygyon e ti nu honeste worshyp wytnesses charge multytude e ti nostra dyscusse yrre gularyte bygamye lewde lewde woman maye taken wytnesse e ti tam seke folke poore folke may compelled come byfore ye iuge bere wytnes iuge may sende wyse men wyt trenth e ti si euery man woman sholde hate false wytnesse god hateth false wytnesse salomon sayth deus odit testem fallacem prouer vi aud euery lyer false wytnesse full gyle sodayne wytnesse dysposeth ordeyneth tonge lyenge redy bere wytnesse byfore auysed dyspeseth hy lye prouer xij salomon sayth false wytnesse shall vnpunysshed speketh lesynges shall perysshe prouer xix ferthermore leue frende ye shall vnderstande ther ben thre maner wytnesses caplm xiij ther wytnesse aboue v knoweth may dysceyued god seeth shall daye dome v iuge wytnesse ego sum iuder et testis iuge wytnesse sayth lorde god ieremie xxix iob sayth heuen wytnesse knoweth couseyll aboue hyghe ther wytnesse within v conscyence saynt poule sayth oure ioye wytnesse conscyence ther wytnesse without v neyghbour creature shall bere wytnesse ayenst v dome byfore ye hyghe iuge amende v tyme deme wel selfe moyses sayd testem inuoco celu et terra calle heuen erthe wytnesse yf ye make ony lykenesse ymage worshyp breke goddes lawe ye shall soone perysshe deutro iiij place sayth thus calle heuen erthe wytnesse haue sette byfore lyfe dethe good euyll blessynge curse therfore chese lyfe ye may lyue loue lorde god obeye voyce clyue hym fayth loue lyfe lengthe dayes herte tourned awaye hym ye wyll lawes worshyppe false goddes saye byfore ye shall soone perysshe deutro xxx therfore leue frende yf wyll syker last dome come sykerly byfore souerayne iuge knoweth muste deme well selfe worlde saynt poule sayth yf demed well selfe dyscussed well lyfe sholde dampned pri ad co rum xi pdiues sholde deme selfe ppauper glose sayth thou shalt thyne owne domesman thy seete shall thyne herte set thy selfe gylty byfore thy selfe domesman thy thought thy conscyence shall thy two wytnesses accuse thy tourmentours sholde drede sorowe maner sholde thy blood wepynge salt teeres whan wytnesse thyne owne conscyence thy thought thou haste demed thy selfe gylty worthy come goddes borde ne heuens blysse sayth glose sekenesse feblenesse sodayne deth falle comonly eester amonges people men eester resceyue vnworthely goddes flesse blood ideo multi infirmi et imbecilles et dormiunt multi per morte prima ad co rum xi euery man fauourable hymselfe owne cause therfore thou shalt haue two assessours whose couseyll thou shalt deme thy selfe tho shall treuthe reasone take treuthe thou make false excusacyon thy synne ne lye thou excuse thyselfe ne excuse thyselfe falsely ne greuously thyne assessour reason wyll accorde yf tho two wytnesses saye thy thought thy conscyence suffyse bere wytnesse ne ful enfourme thy synfull lyf take thrydde wytnesse thy fayth soo lete thy dome stande wytnesse two thre fayth sayth thus fides sine operibus mortua est fayth without good werkes deed alle though byleue crysten man thou lyue crystin man ellys thou art deed soule worthy dye without ende fayth fayleth worde thought deed helpeth blysse anone conscyence mynde shall accorde hym saye thus vseth amys free wyll dye reson without remedye sauynge goddes mercy take hede thy clergy may saue holy wryt clergye saye anima peccatoris mor etur soule synner shall dye also thy clergy may saue yf thou dedely synne thou art bygamus twyus wedded fyrste cryste thy baptym fende assent synne yu art wydowe fro cryste wedded wydowe fende forsaken god pryde wedded begynnynge ye worlde ne truste yu thy dome good contree yf quest comyn x comaudementes whiche thou hast broken two co maudementes charyte ayenst whiche yu haste offended xij artycles fayth ayenst whiche yu haste erred vij dedes mercy whiche yu haste fulfylled thy fyue wyttes whiche yu haste myspended foure cardynall vertues ayenst whiche thou haste trespassed solempne queste xl true wytnesses shal dampne man queller thyne owne soule theef traytour thou haste robbed thyne owne lorde good robberye called al maner mystreatynge mannes good ayenst wyll thou haste robbed cryste precyous soule bought dere blood mysused myspente creature ayenst wyll saynt gregorye sayth omelye thynge take god vse good lyuynge tourne vse wycked lyuynge quicquid ad vsum recipimus vite vsu que conuert mu culpe helthe bodye sent v spende synne wyckednesse fayre weder vayne occupacyon pryde couetyse pea vayne sykernesse plentee vytayles glutonye lecherye solempne queste fourty wolde dampne gylty therfore ther none remedye truly deme thyself yelde gylty take ye mercy god punysshe thy selfe drede sorowe herte put dome goddes iuge thy confessour make amendes dome assent god ayenst yu haste hyghly offended wyll stande ryghtfull dome accepte suche satysfaccon assygneth lawe god yf thou good wyll caplm xiiij thus deme thou thyselfe shalt thou syker dredefull dome whan cryste brother verry god verry man shall come downe deme quycke deed saynt poule sayth shall come downe voyce trumpe saye voyce angelles archangelles whiche shall crye saye surgite mortui venite ad iudicium ryse ye vp ben deed come ye te dome anone twynkelynge eye shall awake longe slepe ryse vp come dome pope prynce emperour kynge lorde lady free bounde ryche poore grete smalle shall awake ryse vp bodye soule ayen knytte togydre voyce shall hydeous dredefull sterne heuen erthe shall begynne quake stone shall ryue deed aryse deth lyf eche man woman answere hymselfe man per attourney iuge cryste lombe mercyfull meke shall lyon dredefull sterne lyon crye abassheth bestes maketh theym stande stylle saue owne whelpes whiche crye reyseth fro deth lyfe voyce cryste daye dome shall arere v deth lyfe whiche voyce shall full dredefull lyue bestely take none hede god ne lawe shall arrest make stande stylle prysoners erth abyde theyr iuge shall charged synne shall wende vp ayenst cryste good shall wende vp mette cryste ben goddes childern voyce shall full swete ful lykynge make soo lyght shall wende vp mete cryste ayre saynt poule sayth childern cryste shall saye venite come ye faders blessyd childern take ye kyngdome heuen ordeyned byfore begynnynge worlde bestyal folke wycked lyuers proude couetouse enuyouse lechoures glotons vengeable folke voyce shall full dredeful fnll bytter whan shall saye discedite maledicti wende ye hen fro ye cursed wretch fyre helle without ende dwelle fende angellys shall sende sory place sory companye without ony remedye ther neuer thondblaste dredefull voyce shall theym shall dampned ther neuer songe mery ne melodye lykyng voyce shal shalbe saued therfore deme well thy selfe thou dampned stande sawe grete queste true wytnesses whiche haue nempned deme thy selfe therafter true domesman thyselfe el yu shalt haue queste ayenst dredefull dome therto angelles archangelles sayntes heuen creature shall bere wytnesse ayenst axe vengeaunce sayth iohn crysostom su illud plangent se omnes tribus terre angelles shal brynge forth crosse spere nayle ye scourge garlonde thornes whiche cryste suffered passyon shall cryste sytte hyghe deme quycke deed shall departe gooe wycked sette good ryght syde wycked lyfte syde shal torne hym wycked lyfte syde shewe theym crosse spere nayles scourge garlonde thornes woudes al fresshe whiche suffered mankynde saye wycked wyse ecce miseri et ingrati quantum vobis sustinui propter vos homo factus sum see ye vnkynde cursed wretch suffered sake whan god kynge kynges lorde lordes neuer wyste woo sake becam man sake suffered beten bounde spateled despysed nayled ye crosse crowned thornes stongen herte spere slayne dyspytous deth ye may see bye endeles deth rau som blood soules bought dere seruyce ye sholde haue done loue yt ye sholde haue shewed loued aboue al creature loued dyde myne owne worshyppe loue putte myselfe sorowe care ye loued lytyll mucke lytyl luste flesshe ye dyd ryghtfulnesse lytyl nought wolde loue whan hongrye ye wolde fede whan thurste ye gaue noo drynke whan naked ye hylde whan sought myne harborowe ye resceyued whan seke pryson ye vysyted therfore wende ye hen fyre helle without ende dwelle fende angelles sayth saynt gregorye thou synfull wretche shalt thou flee may thou ne hyde may yu yf thou appere nedes thou must thou art shent thou shalt haue thynge ayenst aboue thou shalt haue dredefull domesman redy dampne ryght syde thou shalt hane thy wycked werkes accuse lyfte syde foule fendes redy drawe helle byneth yu shalt haue endeles depnes redy swolowe without thou shalt haue worlde fyre redy brenne within thou shalt haue thyn owne conscyence worste gnawynge fretynge without ende wyse man sayth creature shall fyght ayenst v sap v grete clerke sayth crysostomus heuen erthe water sonne mone nyght daye worlde shall stande ayenst v wytnes synnes though alle thynge stylle oure thoughtes conscyence werkes shall accuse v stande wytnesses ayenst v therfore saynt austen omelye su illud estote misericordes sayth thus bretheren take ye hede mercy god harde dome god tyme mercy shall tyme dome god calleth ayen ben tourned awaye fro hym forgyueth ther synnes tourne ayen hym full pacyent abydeth wretche yt men sholde tourne hym saued anone synners tourne ayen god forgyueth synnes yt ben passed byheteth ioyes comyng god yreth monesteth yt ben slowe good dedes conforteth ben dyseased techeth studyouse helpeth fyght ayenst vyces forsaketh man ne woman trauayleth doo well yf calle hym gyueth v sholde gyue ayen hym please hym whan haue offended hym haue gyuen hym ne wherwith queme hym yt take hym tyme mercy ful grete praye false couetyse came periurye false wytnesse murder manslaughter destruccyon kyngdom rede also passyon saynt beatryce yt false couetouse man who name lucre coueyted moche place saynt beatryce couetyse whan moost mery ioconde myddes feste yonge soukynge childe moders arme sayd alowde yt men myght audilu eci lucre thou hast ne thou haste entred falsely place haste thy wyll thou art gyuen myght nought doo whether ryghtfull ryghtfull lefte wyll kepe good man naboth dyde thou spake full late pauper naboth wolde haue kepte uylle faders herytage longeth hym ryght dyscente herytage yf thou kepe ony thynge wyttyngly thy former faders purcha sed falsely kepest thy faders herytage naboth dyde thou kepest mennes herytage whiche neyther ne thy fader ryght therfore thou make restytucyon yu shalt rewe thyne heyres achab dyd heyres whiche loste onely mysgoten naboth murder gyle therto loste theyr lyfe theyr worshyp theyr herytage euer rede ther grete man whiche dyd moche almesse almesse god wolde haue hy saued byfell euenynge romed allone vnder wood syde place ther cam angel ne lykenesse bad hym go wt hym sodaynly togydre depe valey myddes valey depe pytt ful fyre smoderynge medled pytche brymstone full foule stynkynge angell badde man loke pytt loked downe sawe thre galowes standynge fyre ferthest henge man tonge seconde henge man hondes thyrde henge man angell axed hym sawe tolde hym soth sayd angell hangeth tonge thy faders fader whiche purchased place thou dwellest gyle tonge false othes lesynges periurye false wytnesses dyd many men forswere therfore pryncypally punysshed tonge hangeth tonge horryble fyre shall doo without ende wolde make restytucyon hangeth seconde galowes hondes thy fader whiche kepte stylle myghty honde fader amys purchased wolde make restytucyon thyrde galowe whiche hangeth man ben ordeyned yf thou amende make restytucyon anone aungell passeth awaye hym delyuered ayen vnder wood syde next daye sente heyres place made restytucyon wyfe childern full sory sayd vnto hym allas allas ben beggers answered sayd leuer haue begge worlde brynge endelesse payne sawe better v lese place erthe whiche haue ryght lese place heuen blysse without ende pdiues assente well thy speche saye forth thou wylt caplm iiij pauper many harde vengeau ce haue fallen false couety se giezi smyten foule myselrye couetyse made hym selle helthe naman whiche helthe came grace god iiij regu v couetyse iudas solde cryste goddes sone thrytty pen betrayed hym went henge hymselfe tylle bely brast bely brast deuyll hym flewe bare soule hym helle pdiues went fende mouth ppauper mouth hadde touched crystes mouth whan kyssed cryste gyle sayd hayle mayster pdiues thy reason good saye forth thou wylt ppauper also couetyse ananya dnd saphyra wyfe dyed sodayne deth despytouse deth lyed holy goost forsoke theyr moneye saynt peter couetyse nachor stoned deth stalle golde clothe ayenst goddes forbode iosue vij fynde lyfe saynt barlaam tyme archor toke nyghtyngale wolde haue slayne god gaue speche nyghtyngale whiche sayd archer shall profyte slee thou mayst fylle thy wombe soo lytell saue lyfe lett flee shall teche thre wysedomes whiche yf yu kepe well shall moche proufyte archer woudred speche behyght sykerly let flee yf taught hym wysedomes sayd besye take thynge yu myght take thynge lost may recouered ne goten ayen make sorowe thy ge semely soth byleue archer lete nyghtyngale flee whan nyghtyngale vp ayer sayd archer feble couseyll haste thou take yu haste loste grete tresour haue margery stone wombe ostrich egge archer sory prayed nyghtyngale come ayen hym hyght well sayd nyghtyngale wote well thou art fole lore profyteth thou makest moche sorowe thou haste loste yet yu myght gete ayen thou trauayleste take thou myght take ne passe waye passe ouer yu byleuest suche precyous stone body moche ostryches egge bodye halfe moche pdiues purpose ppauper nyghtyngale yt syngeth soo swetely vnderstande cryste goddes sone songe mankynde songes endeles loue nyghtyngale latyn philomena saye englysshe swete louer catholycon sayth sweter louer cryste ther neuer none taughte v many wysdomes whiche taught v thre fyrste bad thou sholdest besye take thynge thou myght take whan bad stele ne coueyte thy neyghbours good wronge lawe sayth hoc solu possumus quod de iure possumus onely may may lawfully therfore yf thou trauayll gete thynge vnlaufully yt yu myght haue lawe house londe worshyp dygnyte yu besyest gete thynge thou myght take therfore wyseman sayth noli laborare vt diteris trauayll thou moche ryche put measure maner thy wysedome thy slyght though yu myghtest gete thynge sleyght sotyltee alwaye take hede ryght lawe ne erigas oculos tuos ad opes quas habere poterissde iure lyfte vp thyne eye sayth salomon rychesses yu myght haue ryghtfully shall make wynges egle flee heuen saye shall flee awaye accuse byfore god thy falsehede thy couetyse prouer xxiij also couetouse folke doo ayenst seconde lesson nyghtyngale cryste ihesus taught v kepe whan lese thynge myshappe aduersyte deth wyfe childern make moche sorowe yt renye god fall full harde sekenesse soule bodye dauyd kyng kepynge wysdome dyd whyle sone laye seke longe hope haue lyfe longe wept fasted prayed lyfe god whan childe deed anone cessed wepynge ete dranke made mery wyste well myght gete hym eyen ij regu xij also couetyse maketh men leue thynge semely soth byleue many stronge lesynges thynge moche desyred soone byleued yt mayster storyes sayth moche couetouse folke desyren haue moche thynge yt haue noo ryght therfore byleue many falle tale assenten falsehede couetouse false accorden soone gydre yf false man come telle couetouse man false tale wynnynge telleth hym hath ryght thynge byleueth hym soone neuer false therfor nyghtyngale blessyd ihesus sayd qui cito credit leuis est corde soone byleueth lyght herte full chaungeable vertue vyce treuth falsenesse charyte couetyse et minorabi soone byleueth shall lessed worshyp lytyll set soone byleuynge lesynges bryngeth people moche folye maketh men begynne playes bryges one neyghbour hate hnsbonde hate wyfe wyf hyr husbonde fader sone sone fad moder hyr doughter brother syster hath brought englonde bytter balys therfore wyse man sayth non omni verbo credas byleue euery worde ecclxiiij yt byleueth soone lesynges worde loue fayth wawe wynde therfore grete clerke seneca sayth epistle noo wyse man byleueth ony newe tale lyghtly caplm v also rede holy wryt numeri xxij balaam false prophete wolde haue cursed goddes people couetyse gyftes whiche balaa kyng moab profered notwithstandynge yt god forbad hym badde hym come wherfor rode kyng balaa asse yt rode vndername hym hurte fote ayenst walle asse sawe angel standynge wt swerde drawen ayenst hym waye therfor asse fledde yt waye yt felde balaam wroth smote asse full harde wt staffe bare waye asse cam strayt waye bytwene two walles sawe also angell ayenst hym dred fledde syde bare balaam ayenst walle hurte fote ayenst walle balaam bette asse full euyll soone angell stode ayenst hym strayt waye yt asse myght flee ony syde felle downe wolde ferther efte smote asse god opened ass mouthe sayd balaam haue ayenst betest thou thyrde tyme haue alwaye thy beest thou haste alwaye roden serued neuer thus tyll god opened eyen balaam sawe angell standynge ayenst hym naked swerde whiche repreued hym false couetyse wycked purpose bete asse without gylte sayd asse gone waye sholde ellys haue slayne hym waye ayenst plesauce god pdiues betokeneth tale ppau balaam saye englysshe deuourer people troubelour folke interpretat deuorans pplm et turban gentem therfore balaam betokeneth false couetyse worlde whiche deuoureth poore people troubled euery nacyon nyghe debate worlde myne thyne therfore sayd phylosopher tolle duo verba meu et tuum et totus mundus erit pace put worlde two wordes myne thyne worlde shall pea balaam fyrst prophecye worshypped goddes people prophecyed moche prosperyte co pelled myght god saye laste shrewde couseyll gaue balaac haue gyftes desceyued goddes people brought theym lecherye ydolatrye offende god wherfore foure twenty thousande goddes people slayne prynces people hanged vpon gebettes ayenst sonne byddynge god ryght couetyse worlde fyrste putteth men hope grete prosperyte byheteth welth worshyp see sayth couety se suche clerke may spende moche yere yet poore mane sone thou art good herte suche thou myght soo couetyse putteth example knyghtes marchauntes prelate lordes ladyes yf thou haue rychesse sayth couety se thou may moche almesse haue many preestes praye purgatory beware suche byhestes fende worldely couety se ben desceyue brynge glotonye lecherye ydolatrye balaam brought goddes people shenshyp wolde make truste thy good thy god thynge man woman loueth moost setteth herte moost therin god saynt ierom sayth therfor saynt poule sayth auaryce seruage mawnetrye golde god couetouse man doth moost worshyp whiche fals god betokened ymage golde xl cubytes hyght vi brede whiche kyng nabugodono sor reysed vp felde durayn compelled men worshyp wolde worshyp dyd put theym ouen ful fyre token worshypeth worlde false god golde false couetyse gyueth tale worlde wyll obeye false couetyse serue gyle falsehede periurye lyue treuth charyte man shal haue moche woo worlde therfor saynt poule sayth yt wyll lyue mekely goodly cryste shall suffre moche trybulacyon worlde therfor saynt gregory sayth worlde forneys ouen trye goddes childern anguysshe try ulacyon beware byhestes couetyse fayre byhestes make sottes blythe wyll entryke dette synne shal full harde escape brynge dye dedly synne yf thou dye dedely synne golde vnder cope heuen though thyne ne preestes vnder sonne maye helpe therfor saynt poule sayth qui vo lunt diuites fieri incidut temptaco ne et laqueu dyaboli coueyte ryche worlde fall harde temptacons fendes snare wycked desyres vnprouffytable full noyous whiche drenche men deth helle brynge perdycon fayth rote euyll couetyse prima ad thi vi caplm vi diues wene men myght holpen ryche ss deth ppauper shall holpen theyr good theyr deth deserue theyr lyfe holpen theyr rychesses ther deth doo almesse theyr astate spende well goodes god hath sente theym paye well theyr dettes doo suche good dedes kepe wel theym dedely synne theyr lyues ende namely thus sayth saynt austen glosa prima ad thessalo quarto su illud nolumus vos ignorare de dormientibus therfore beware take hede thre warnynges tokenes god gaue balaam flee swerde fyrste asse went waye hurte fote dyseased bodye laste felle downe vnder hym wolde ferther bere hym asse vnderstande welth worlde standeth pryncypaly rychesses bodely helth whiche bereth man vp worlde asse bare balaam beware ryght asse full dulle beest whan man hath moost nede moost haste iourney wyll go owne luste desceyueth mayster ryght worldely welth desceyueth truste therin fayleth nede asse worldely welth fyrst goth waye whan god sendeth man aduersyte cause trauayle goth forth wolde ne wende sholde whan neth wynne leseth spedeth wende spede weneth fynde frendes fyndeth enemyes caas yf wyll passe see wynde ayenst hym dryueth hym waye yf plete slyght putteth hym purpose wende spede moneth shall spede yere perauenture neuer brynge cause right waye wolde haue whan asse gothe waye take hede thy waye thy purpose yf thy waye purpose ayenst pleasauce god waye balaam wende ayen cesse thyn euyll purpose yf de ayenst pleasaunce god dyspose pacyence thanke god al take hede angell sayd balaam asse sayd ne hadde gone waye hadde slayne welthe worlde wente tyme oute waye aduersyte sekenesse ellys sholde cause moche folke dethe bothe bodely goostly yf man hadde alwaye welthe wyll worlde sholde gyue noo tale god ne man seconde token hurte fote dyseased bodye whan god sendeth man sekenesse casteth hym downe bedde maketh hym feble foot may bere hym take thou hede thy waye thy lyfe yf ought contrarye god yf amendeth thrydde token asse fell downe vnder foot strayt waye wolde ferther bere hym strayt waye narowe paas deth man may flee welth worlde lykened asse falleth downe grounde wyll lenger bere man vpon worlde passeth helth welth luste flesshe therfore whan thou comest poynt take hede thy waye thy lyfe yf contrarye god amende euer thou wylt flee goddes swerde ryche sse welthe worlde lykened iogulours horse fynde tyme came proude getter stable founde mynstralles horse standynge poore namely euyll goten good soone playeth flectamus genu haue mysgoten myspurchace withholdynge dette false executorye mycherye robberye therfore comon prouerbe de male quesitis vix gaudet tercius busshe goth tyll naked ryght thornes false rychesses suche dettes shall take thy flese fro saye thy true catell yf yu ony haue soo thou shalt haue ryght nought helpe thyselfe tyll whan yu shalt go naked good haue lesse nought therfor sayth grete clerke tulli liij de officijs noo thynge saueth comonte fayth fayth may sayth men wyll paye theyr dettes iij boke de officijs sayth synne ayenst kynde welth floures anone whele tourned downe ayen greter age pouerte sekenesse feblenesse tyll laste falleth whele dyeth lyeth clotte erthe walle therfore whele fortune wryten verse regnabo regno regnaui su sine regno man youth whan towarde hope welth sayth regnabo shall reygne whan myddel age hath worlde wyll sytteth whele sayth pryde regno reygne aboue anone whele tourneth downewarde anone cometh age sekenesse feblenesse losse catell aduersyte may saye regnaui haue reygned somtyme man whan lyeth deynge may saye sum sine regno without kyngdome reygne kyngdome welth done also whele fortune one syde anone syde ben daye mane frendes stande syde helpe hym next daye shall enemyes stande ayenst hym wt aduersarye whele speketh dauyd circuitu impij ambulant wycked couetouse folke go whele posuisti man neuer grete worlde haue wynde ne mouth neuer wel wt hym bere name prayse flater hym though na e sprynge neuer wyde bere hym neuer hygh pryde solempne myghty man dare quycche ayenst ne deed passed fadeth wayes saye lyuynge iacobi also worldely welth lykened shadowe alwaye passyng lyuynge worlde passynge wantynge lyght heuen blysse myddes daye whan sonne hyghest shadowe shortest ryght whan man fro hym sooner harder shall falle bnt yf loke wel foot waye may kepe left though fall shall take grete harme ryght fareth lyfe worlde slyder yt ther myght neuer man ne woman passe wayt laste slydeth selfe ye gyue dyenge therfore ye gyue ye may bere therfore moder whyle ye lyue haue helth bodye gyue god ye haue caplm xi whan man wyll hyself whyle may though executours attorney nought hym grete woudre eche man woman moost holden hymselfe fareth ofte hem dyed theyr executours dyd one two fooles dwelled lordes courte one foole sage naturell foole byfell daye came gydre kabehouse whan folke ouen ouen glowynge hote sayde foole sage natural foole whether ouen hote semeth wyll assaye sayd ye sayd foole sage whiche v shall go ouen fyrste assaye sayd naturell foole shall goo thou shalte haue bolle full water stande ouens mouth yf fele hete crye caste caste anone caste water quenche fyre shall done sayd foole naturell foole toke foole sage bolle full water honde wente crepte ouen anone beganne brenne anone cryed caste caste whan foole sawe foly laughed enterely foly vnnethes myght stonde fete foole ouen cryed caste man caste brenne deth foole answered brene yu yf brenne wylt dye yf thou dye wylt laugh may caste foole brent deth ye ouen tho two fooles vnderstaude men dye theyr false executours ben fooles executours ben grete fooles bynde theym helle payne theyr falsehede dye ben fooles truste men themself whan shall crepe purgatorye hoter ony ouen take theyr executours bolle full water theyr honde saye golde syluer rychesses almesse almesdede mass syngynge holy prayer namely ye frendes honde god full harde hath touched whan fynde helpe sholde helpe axe vengeauce nyght daye grete clerke turpin de gest karoli telleth yt kyng charles wt hym knyght oost man good doo whan thrytty dayes passed nyght folowynge knyght apperyd slepe neuewe axed hym done bad hym excused dyuer se besynesses fayned hadde axed eme fared answered sayd shall telle fare thou shalt fare alle thrytty dayes haue ben purgatorye suffred ful moche woo payne defaute helpe thanke god passed purgatorye goo vp heuens blysse without ende thou woldest helpe badde therfore daye mydmorowe thou shalt dye goo helle without ende next daye folowynge rode oost horse tolde dremes felowes iape mydmorowe came sodaynly blake skye thondre lyghtnynge grete nombre fendes lykenesse rauens rokes hent hym deed fyndeth fewe frendes caplm xij pauper rede vita barla ther ryche man whiche iij frendes fyrste frende seconde loued herte thyrde frende loued lytell nought man felle suche daunger ayenst kyng yt good forfetted eschetyd ye kyng hymselfe wened haue ben slayn wente fyrste frende yt loued soo moche praynge hym helpe yt wolde go kyng speke hy saue lyfe yf myght answerd sayd fare well faue knowe haue felowes frendes ynough haue myrtes solace nathelesse yf thou slayne shall gyue shete burye went seconde frende loued soo moche praynge hym also helpe excused hym sayd praye haue excused besye may atende yet olde felaushyp shall go waye yate went thyrde frende loued lytel prayed hym helpe sayd leue frende ashamed speke haue ben ful vnkynde lytell loue shewed praye haue reuth goddes sake helpe pellycane al foules moost chere ouer byrdes moost loueth ther grete enmyte bytwene adder wherfor adder wayteth whan pellycane neste seke mete byrdes goth neste pellycane styngeth byrdes enuenemeth sleeth whan pellycane cometh ayen fyndeth byrdes thus slayn maketh moche sorowe mone waye kynde thre dayes thre nyght morneth deth byrdes thyrde dayes ende setteth hym ayen ouer byrdes bylle smyteth hymselfe syde letteth blood falle downe byrdes anone blode toucheth byrdes anon waye kynde vertue ye blood quycken ayen rysen deth lyfe pellycane loueth well byrdes vnderstande cryste ihesu goddes sone loueth mannes soule woman euer dyd pellycane byrdes sayth hymselfe similis factus su pellicano solitudinis made lyke pellycane deserte byrdes vnde adam eue mankynde nest vnderstande blysse paradyse right byrdes brought forth nest mankynde begynnynge brought forth paradyse adder vnderstande fende whiche appered lyknes adder eue stange full euyl adam also wt wycked fondynge slewe bodye soule slewe also slewe al mankynde yf adam synned sholde neuer haue dyed ne haue wyst woo wherfore pellycane ihesu cryste seynge myscheef mankynde fall gyle fende ruth mankynde grete loue makynde sayt poul sayth auentysshed hyselfe toke flesshe blood mayden mary bycam man lykenesse seruaut manhede kynde suffered taken boude beten forspyted dispysed byscorged pyler crowned thornes nayled tree hondes foot hanged crosse theef amonges theues stonge herte sharpe spere dyed bytter deth gylt gylt dyd neuer amys worde ne dede saynt peter sayth pystle thus loue yt ben hym ful vnkynde shed precyous blood euery parte blysfull bodye born mayden inner hert blood shed wasshe v fro synnes reyse v fro deth synne lyfe grace fro bodely deth lyf endles blysse therfore saynt iohn sayth dilexit no lauit no pccis n sanguie suo apoc loued v moche yt wasshed v fro synnes wt precyous blood loue droue hym downe fro heuen erth loue led hy maydens bosom brought hym wycked worlde loue boude hy cradel wonde hy cloutes ful poore layd hy oxe stalle loue helde hy sorowe care honger thryst moche trauayl xxxij yere last loue toke hy boude hy set hy barre byfore synful iustyce ponce pylate loue layd crosse nayled hy tree loue led hy deth cleef hert two whose loue leue frende forsoth loue synful wretch yt neuer dyd hy good offended hym nyght day ben hym ful vnkynde therfor may well saye wordes salomon sayd fortis e vt mors dilectio viij loue stronge deth ye forsoth moche strenger deth loue led lyfe deth neuer myght dye waye kynde loue made hym dye mankynde sayth salomon brondes loue ben brondes fyre flammes loue shewed mankynde also loue ought shewe ryght hete sonne lyght whan shyneth fyre house wasteth fyre quencheth loue god endelesse charyte passyon yf shone mane soule hete sholde quenche waste brondes fyre lecherye brennynge mannes soule foule luste wycked desyre therfore sayth euery crysten soule one vt signaculu su cor tuu viij set token vpon thyn herte saynt poul sayth spu abulate desideria carnis ficiet ad gala v go ye holy goost yt called welle goostly fyre ye shal desyre flesshe deuocon mynde crystus passyon best remedy ayenst temptacon lechery caplm iiij also good remedye man thynke deth freelte bytter paynes helle euer lastynge hygh offence god endeles ioyes lese yf assent lecherye therfore salomon sayth memorare nouissima tua eternu peccabis eccl vij thynke thy laste thynges yu shalt neuer doo synne eche man woman sholde beware neyther nyce contenau ce ne foly speche ne nyce araye body styre ony man woma lecherye though resonable arraye honeste comended man woman theyr astate ruled goddaes lawe reason muste well ware suche arraye falle pryde ne lecherye ne styre lecherye wyllynge wetynge rede vitas patrum ther holy woman whose name alexandre full fayre woman whan herde saye man fallen harde temptacon lecherye bycau se beaute closed house wolde neuer see man ne come yt house toke lyuynge smalle wyked men axed dyde saye hadde leuer shytte herselfe quyck graue harme ony soule god made lykenesse bought soo dere precyous blood rede also lyfe saynt bryde yt man wolde haue wedded beaute prayed god wolde sen blemysshynge face wherby mannes temptacyon myght cese anone one eye braste hede wherfore fader made nune woman vnable worlde wha made nune forsaken worlde anone eye syght ayen thus sholde wymen besely kepe chastyte clennesse maydens chastyte maydenhode wydowes chastyte wydowehode wyues chastyte wedloke kepe ther bodye truly theyr husbondes husbo de truly theyr wyues forsoth dedely synne man desyre mannes wyfe mayden doughter flesshely luste moche dedely synne oppresse defoule lye caplm v diues saynt poule sayth flesshe desyreth couey seth alwaye ayenst soule full harde withstande lustes desyres ppauper therfore man sholde gouerne chastyse bodye good man armes gouerneth chastysed horse iob sayth lyuynge vpon erth knyghthode fyghtyng ayenst fende worlde flesshe iob vij batayle bodye horse whiche muste chastyse rule knyght dooth horse yf horse proude euyl tached may lyghtly lese mayster becau se deth yf tame mayster well tached shall hym worshyp helpe nede case saue lyfe thre thynges ben nedeful knyght rule wel horse muste haue brydel sadel two spore brydel vnder stande abstynence trauayle whiche flesshe muste refrayned fro lustes euyll tacches whan begynneth wexe proude wynsynge kykyng ayenst mayster yt soule yf ouer proude rebell mayster muste haue sharpe brydel sharpe abstynence harde trauayle yf meke tretable gyue hym smothe brydel easy abstynence comon trauayle raynes thy brydel sholde two partes temporau ce yt saye neyther moch ne lytel knyt togydre knot gode discrecon thyn shal go ryght forth waye lyfe bere heuenly blysse hou gyue thy flesshe moche drynke ease wyll thy may ter slee yf thou gyue lytell shall feble fayle nede let thy iourneye sadell thyn horse shall pacyence mekenesse thou pacyente adnersyte sekenesse yt yu folowe grutchynges sterynges thy flesshe steroppes thy sadell sholde lowenesse sadnesse lowenesse ayenst pryde sadnesse ayenst worlde flesshe thou sory wo ne gladde wele ne welfare sytte sadely thy sadell kepe well thy steroppes pryde ne wrathe sekenesse aduersyte let thy horse caste downe sadel pacyence syt faste vertue goostly strength kepe thy soule sadel pacyence cryste byddeth gospell whan sayth paciencia vra possidebi aias vras ye shall kepe soules pacyence sadell maketh horse semely plesaut syght pacyence maketh man plesaut syght god men maketh haue loue euery co pany ben wrath inpacyence hastynes maketh vnplesaut without loue sadel god spake caym whan wroth wt brother abel sayd god art yu wroth thy face thy fallen fallen sadell pacyence yf yu well yu shalt resceyue good mede yf yu euyll anone thy synne cometh yate punysshed desyre synne shal vnder thy power horse vnder knyght thou shalt lorde therof yf thou wylt gen iiij caym mysgouernauce hors felle sadel pacyence manslaughter brod wolde kepe hy sadel pacyence ne refrayne wycked desyre flesshe therfore god cursed hy fyrst men therfore leue frende kepe well sadel pacyence let angre ne losse catell ne deth frendes none aduersyte trybula cyon sekenesse vnsadel pacyence sytte ye fast iob dyd saye ye sayd whan hadde loste good childern slayne hymselfe smyten harde sekenesse horryble foule sayd thus yf haue taken good thynges goddes honde sholde suffre wyked thynges paynfull sond god yaue god hath taken awaye god wyll done blessyd lordes name iobietijca thus sytte ye sadely sadell pacyence rule ye horse brydell abstynence reynes temperau ce yf horse dulle goddes way pryke hym two spore ben diede helle payne loue god heuen blysse drede loue compelle ye hors hye forth goddes waye let horse flesshe carnalle ease welfare ne feble mysfa e ouertrauayle caplm vi mayster kynde liiiij de qualitate elementari telleth ther byrde called bernake byrde wexeth tree ouer water longe hanged tree deed anon louseth tree falleth downe water anone quykeneth swymmeth forthe byrde sayth hath lytell flesse lesse blood tree vnderstande mankynde came al adam eue tree brau ches come al rote byneth byrde vnderstande euery man woman whiche whan fyrst born theyr moder deed orygynal synne adam able lyf grace ne blysse saynt poule sayth ben born childern wrath deth anone falle stone water baptyme ben baptysed anon resceyue ly grace able lyf heuen blysse yf kepe v besely blood synne carnalyte bodye desytes flesshe saynt peter byddeth v abstinete vos carnali bus desiderijs que militat aduersus aiam petri ij absteyne ye flesshely desyres yt fyght ayenst soule moche iob sayth mannes lyf vpon erth knyghthode fyghtyng ayenst goostly enemyes milicia e vi ta hois su terra iob vij therfore nedefull euery crysten man gouerne wel horse bodye haue sayd ouer saynt poule sayth mnste arme hy goostley armure ayenst dyntes dartes fendes temptacyon saynt poule sayth ad eph vi fyghtynge ayenst wycked spyrytes derkenesses whiche prynces power gouernours synfull men therfore sayth arme ye armure god ye may withstande busshement slyghtes deuyll stande parfyght al thynges stande ye sayth treuth gyrde ye lendes gyrdel chastyte ye habergeon ryght fulnesse shoe ye foot dyghtynge gospell pea thynges take ye shelde fayth whiche ye may quenche al brennynge dartes wycked fende take ye basynet helth swerde holy goost goddes worde whiche sayth another place sharper ony two egged swerde ad hebre iiij almaner prayer besechynge praye ye euery tyme alwaye spiryte wake ye alwaye maner besynesse thus saynt poule lykenesse bodely armure techeth v goostly armure techeth v well arme lendes vertue chastyte whan byddeth v gyrde well lendes byddeth v habergeon ryghtfulnesse defence bodye soule ryght yelde god euery creature yt longeth hym soueraynes felowes sugettes theym ben byfore v paste worlde almesse gyuynge yeldynge dettes ben deed theym ben behynde v come sauynge theyr ryght theyr due herytage thus arme v behynde byfore euery syde habergeon ryghtfulnesse ryght habergeon euery rynge accordeth wt knytt sholde ryghtfulnes accorde gydre knytt gydre yt ryght soo yt man ne woman wronge yf moche ryght fauour one hyndrynge others ryght rynges haberge ryghtfulnes accorde ne well knytt gydre ther hole wherby fende may hurte soule also byddeth v arme foot legges legge harneys goostly pouerte yt withdrawe hertes affeccyons erthely thynges set loue moche erthly thynges ne worldely goodes stryue plete noo worldely goodes nede compell v therto seke lyue pea men yf may thus arme v goostly poue te legges foot saye loue affeccons ayenst temptacyons false couetyse therfore byddeth v shoe foot dyghtynge
