shyne dayene lyght mone shal shyne nyght thy lorde god cryst ihesus yt bought dere shal lyght without ende thy god shal thy ioye thy sonne shall neuer go downe thy shal neuer wayne thy lorde god shall thy lyght without ende dayes thy sorowe worlde shall ended god shall wype awaye teres eyen sayntes ther shalbe wepynge cryeng hongre thrust sorow wo dyseases byfore ben past come cyte ye people cyte shal good ryghtful shal shrewe bryger lechour wycked lyuer entre cyte euery man woman shall shyne bryght sonne whan many sonnes ben gadred gydre companye wt hygh sonne ryghtfulnes cryst ihesus whiche sayth ye gospell ego su lux mudi io viij lyght worlde shall fayre company blysfull company god brynge v therto sonne shall vij tymes brygh er mone bryght sonne sonne shal stande ye eest alwaye styll mone west alwaye shynynge without wanyng yt synful soules dampned helle vnd therth shall confort haue neyther sonne ne mone kyngdome cyte wynde storme tempest thondre lyghtnyng rayne hayl frost ne snowe hete colde ther skyes cloudes let lyght alwaye mery somer alwaye bryght daye cyte al men wymen ben free kyng cyte axeth presautes ne gyftes man ne woman theyr hertes theyr loue yt fare well putteth man ne woman trauayle wyl yt rest pea ease ony man woman desyreth haue gyueth anone axeth rente trybute seruyce none homage good loue good herte loue hym ioye myrth gladnesse gyueth v axeth v gyue thy selfe blysse yu shalt haue blysse pryce axeth none blysse may bought loue charyte cyte shall euery man woman haue grete lordshyp al shall haue place ynough without enuye al kynges quenes moche desyre ther shall pletynge lordshyd londe ther shall none enuye euery man woman glad others welfare ther shal wo dysease endelesse ioye welth endelesse helth herynge swete songe melodye syght endeles fayrnesse tastynge smellynge endelesse swetene sse felynge endelesse lykynge without woo caplm xi cyte speketh saynt iohan boke goddes preuytees xxi ca sayth thus angell ledde spiryte vysyon full hygh hylle full grete shewed holy cyte ierusalem ordeyned god hauynge bryghtnesse beaute god lyght cyte lyke precyous stone spis crystel whiche stone betokeneth cryste sonne ryghtwysnesse whiche sayth gospell ego su lux mudi io viij lyght worlde cyte walle ull hygh xij yates eche yate xij angelles redye porter lede good soules yates wryten name xij kynredes israel saye yt shall saued able see god face name al yt shall saued ben regystred boke lyfe heuen redy wryten yates heuen ayenst comynge token shall welcome syker blysse yf ur deuour cyte stode square thre yates cest thre north thre south thre west token foure partes worlde saye euery parte worlde soules entre heuen blysse yonge olde ryche poore fayth holy trynyte betokened thre ya e yonge folke ben vnderstande eest daye begynneth olde folke weste daye endeth ryche folke south poore folke north yt cot moost sharpe bareyne walle cyte set grouded xij precyo stone fyrste iaspis ij saphirus iij calcidoni iiij smaragdus v sardenix vi sardinus vij crisolitus viij berillus ix topasius x crisopassus xi iacinct xij amati stus tho stone wryten name xij apostle goddes lombe walle made precyous stone yates made saphires smaragdes tobye sayth boke xiij ca saynt iohn sayth euery yate margaryte margery stone stretes ye cyte clene golde clere glasse tobye sayth stretes cyte paued wt ful whyte clene stone always siretes songe alleluya whiche songe coude neuer clerke well declare ne expowne vtterest ioye myrth melodye gladnesse may noo tonge telle ne herte thynke ne honde wryte ne wytte deuyse declare cyte saynt iohn sawe temple almyghty goddes lombe cryste ihesus verry god man temple cyte cyte sayth saynt iohn nedeth neyther sonne ne mone bryghtnesse god welle lyght sonne ryghtfulnesse illumyneth cyte lombe cryste ihesus lanterne lyght cyte nacyons people shall go lyght cyte brynge theyr nobley theyr blysse theyr worshyp cyte yates cyte shall neuer shytte ther shal nyght alwaye daye alwaye somer neuer wynter cyte shall come noo foule thynge false lyer forswerer ne none dooth abhomynacon dedely synne ther shall man entre ben wryten boke lyf lyf lombe cryste ihesus yt bought v dere blood caplm xij sayd grete clerke doctor de lyra xij precyo stone whiche cyte grounded whiche stone name xij apostle wryten ben vnderstande xij artycles fayth whiche xij apostle gadred one crede whiche xij artycles saluacyon set grounded therfore saynt poule sayth fide statis stande ye fayth oure fayth groude saluacon xij yates ben vnderstande ten comasidemente two comaudementes charyte whiche yates cryste sayth si vi ad vitam ingredi serua mandata math xix yf thou wylt entre lyfe blysful cyte noman dyeth kepe thou comaudementes scrypture wryten euery yate cyte token cyte cometh noo man ne woman b kepers goddes comaudementes comau dementes ben yates heuen whiche muste entre ben also waye ledynge yate heuen therfore dauyd sayth viam mandatoabrum tuoabrum cucurri cu di latasti cor meu po c xviij ranne waye commaundementes whan thou madest myne rrte large charyte whan men strayte brest false couetyse nygardshyp may well renne waye goddes byhestes fals couetyse byndeth theym soo strayt herte haue noo lykynge goddes byhestes therfor dauyd sayd deduc dne semita mada toabrum tuoabrum qr ipam volui inclina cormeu deus testimonia tua aet auaricia po c xviij lorde lede yu pathe thy comaudementes desyre wyll goo waye bowe myne herte thy wytnessynges thy comau deme auaryce couetyse thus leue frende holy wrytt holy men declare blysse heuen thynges vysyble yt may see eye lede v knowynge blysse yt may see wt bodely eye whyle lyue londe deth leue frende byleue ye forsoth ther hondred thousande thousande folde blysse ony tonge may telle ony herte thynke caplm xiij diues yf men hadde sadde fayth haue suche blysse theyr good dedes ther wolde man ne woman mys drede lese blysse ppauper fareth folke born pryson ye wycked worlde doth childe born depe derke pytte pryson whan falleth woman childe put pryson moder knoweth welfare pryson moche sorowe care longeth full moche pryson ayen welfare childe born myscheef pryson neuer hadde knowynge better fare gyueth lytell tale myscheue pryson aslonge hath moder hym sustenau ce though full feble maketh sorowe ne care longeth better fare knoweth better yf moder tell hym ioye welfare pryson sonne mone sterres fayre floures spryngynge vpon erthe byrdes syngynge myrthe melodye ryche arraye lordes ladyes welth yt pryson hyr tale dreme childe byleueth therfore longeth therafter wyll blysse welfare speketh forsake moder ne feble fare yt hath byleueth yet moder telleth childe childe one pryson sawe welth myrth welfare whiche moder tolde hym wolde full sory go ayen pryson lyue moder lyfe pryson fyrst lykynge ynough hy sholde full bytter sholde neuer haue ioye ne reste herte tyll came ayen yt welfare yt sawe pryson ryght thus folke worlde borne brought forth sorowe care moche trauayl pryson worlde haue moche loue lykynge theyr erthly moder ther co panye saye erth erthely thynges erth moder al haue lykynge heuenly thynges ne longe therafter yet theyr gostly moder holy chirche ther goostly fader god selfe fader telleth blysse heuen dreme moders tale childe pryson haue noo sad fayth therin though mod holy chirche telleth v thoughe childe byleue suche welfare pryson welfare neuer lesse though erthely couetouse men haue lykynge erth erthly thynges byleue suche blysse heuen yet ther suche blysse neuer lesse theyr false byleue one sene assayed lytell blysse al ioye lykynge yt haue worlde erthly thynges sholde full grete bytternesse full sorowe care example haue saynt peter cryste ledde vpon hylle thabor saynt iohn saynt iames shewed lytell blysse manhode face shone bryght sonne clothes whyte snowe moyses hely appered hym grete blysse magestee peter sayd lorde ihesu lorde good v make thre tabernacle one moyses hely let v dwelle luce ix anone syght lytel blysse forgat al blysse worlde cared neyther mete drynke ne clothynge hym thought myght haue lyued without ende blysfull syght company also whan saynt poule rauysshed heuen seen vysyon god afterwarde lyf worlde payne moche longed ayen yt blysse therfore sayd infelix ego quis liberabit demorte coris hui rovij vnsely man shall delyuer fro deth body coueyte departed soule bodye without ende cryste moyses wt god mout synay xl dayes xl nyghtes metelesse drynkeles fedd speche god presence yet sawe lytell blysse able see blysse ne noman lyuynge worlde god sayd hym tyme leue frende deth yf kepe well goddes commaundementes amende mysdedes lyfe shal see grete blysse whiche neither peter ne poule ne moyses myght see erthe shalbe syker blysse without ende whiche blysse saynt poule sayth none erthely eye may see ne ere ne herte thynke ne wytte
